11a3(1): kun tu bzang po thams cad don// byang chub sems ni rab bskor ba// byang chub spyod pa rdo rje che// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs dag pa// sku dang gausung thugs rdo rje 
11a4(1): 'dzin// sangs rgyas byang chub rab ston pa// byang chub sems la phyag 'tshal lo// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cod kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las/ byang chub kyi sems kyi 
11a5(1): le'u ste gnyis pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 
11a6(1): 'gro ba'i sprin bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ rdo rje bkod pa zhes bya ba ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u 'di gsungs so// oM shu n+ya ta gnya' na badz+ra swa b+hA wa ad ma ko&haM// na mkha'i dbyis 
11a7(1): kyi dbus gnas par// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor bsgom pa ni// 'od zer sprin gyi tshogs chen po// sangs rgyas 'bar ba'i 'od dang mnyam// 'od zer sna lngas kun tu khyab// kun nas yongs su zlum pa 
11b1(1): ste// gzungs kyi lha mo lnga la sogs// 'dod pa'i yon tan lnga yis khyab// mchod pa rnam pa lngas brgyan pa// mdor na de ltar bsgoms nas su// gzugs ni dbus su bsgom par bya// rnam par snang 
11b2(1): mdzad phyag rgya che// sku gsung thugs kyis mtshan pa'o// sku gsung thugs ni rdo rje yis// phyag rgya 'am yang na bsgom par bya// bsdus dang gcig tu sbyor ba yis// tshogs gnyis dang ni ldan pa yis// mi 
11b3(1): skyod pa'i rgya mchog dang // dkon mchog dpal gyi rgya chen dang // tshe dpag med kyi 'od byed dang // thogs med grub pa'i rgya chen rnams// sangs rgyas dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// sku gsung thugs kyi rdo 
11b4(1): rje can// in tra ni li kha dog 'dral// rab 'bar phyag na rdo rje bsnams// rnam paro rtsigs la 'jigs 'jigs lta// shel dang zla ba'i 'od 'dra ba// thor tsugs cod pon gyis brgyan pa// rab 'bar 
11b5(1): phyag na 'khor lo bsnams// sna tshogs rgyan gyis mdzes par brgyan// 'dzam bu chu bo'i gser 'od 'dra// sangs rgyas sprin gyis kun tu 'khrigs// de'i phyag na rdo rje che// rtse mo dag pa rnam par 
11b6(1): bsgom// ma ra ta ga'i 'od 'dra ba// rdo rje 'bar bas rnam par brgyan// kun tu 'bar ba'i sprin gyis khyab// phyag na rin chen rnam par bsgoms// pad+ma ra ga'i mdog 'dra ba// gtso bo 'dod chags 
11b7(1): 'bar ba mnga'// rab 'bar phyag na pad+ma bsnams// 'dod chags rdo rje can bsgoms bya// 'od zer lnga'i 'od 'dra'i sku// gdon mi za ba rdo rje can// zhi ba phyag na ral gri bsnams// sangs rgyas 
12a1(1): dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje/ de bzhin gshegs pa chos kyi dbyings kyi ngo 
12a2(1): bo nyid rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sku dang gsung dang thugs byin gyis rlob pa zhes bya ba'i sngags 'di gsungs so// oM d+haR+Sha d+ha ra du sA b+ha wa ad ma ko haM// rin chen chen 
12a3(1): bo kha dog lnga// nyungs kar gyi ni 'bru tshad tsam// sna'i rtse mor nan tan du// rnal 'byor pa'i rtag tu bsgom// rin cheni rten par gyur nas spro// brtan par ma gyur yong mi spro// sangs rgyas 'bar ba 
12a4(1): 'dra ba'i 'od// mchog rnams sprin rnams spro bar bya// 'khor lo rdo rje rin chen dang // pad+ma ral gri mtshon cha 'dzin// byang chub sems dpa' sprin chen rnams// spro ba'i bdag nyid can gyi spro// 
12a5(1): na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// rdo rje dkyil 'khor bri bar bya// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor dbus gnas par// 'khor lo dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor 'dra bar 
12a6(1): ni/ pad+ma zlos pa bsgom par bya// rin chen dkyil 'khor 'dra ba ni// rin chen brtson pas bsgom par bya// sbyor ba'i dkyil 'khor las byung ba// nam mkha' 'dra bar bri bar bya// 'di dag sangs 
12a7(1): rgyas rab kyi mchog/ sku gsung thugs ni bsgoms pa yis// dkyil 'khor rdo rje las byung ba// thams cad mkhyen pa'i tshul thob pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang 
12b1(1): thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las/ rdo rje bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin gyi le'u ste gsum pa'o// / de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 
12b2(1): yang 'dus nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi bdag po la/ bstod pa'i rgyal po 'di gsol ba btab po// de bzhin gshegs pa kun bzhi la/ 
12b3(1): de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi gnas// chos kun bdag med pa yi mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// mtshan rnams thams cad yang dag rdzogs// mtshan min thams cad yang dag spangs/ 
12b4(1): kun tu bzang po'i sku mchog/ dkyil 'khor dam pa bshad du gsol// sems can kun gyi sems chen po// rang bzhin dag cing dri ma med// kun bzang thugs mchog kha lo sgyur// dkyil 'khor 
12b5(1): dam pa bshad du gsol// de nas ston pa rdo rje 'dzin// 'jig rten gsum po khams gsum pa// 'jig rten gsum mchog rdo rje gtso// 'jig rten gsum mchog pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi 
12b6(1): gnas// de bzhin gshegs pa kun gyi thugs// thugs kyi dkyil rab 'dra ba// dkyil 'khor rab tu nyams dga' bshad// de nas thugs kyi dkyil 'khor mchog/ thugs kyi rdo rje rab 'dra ba// sku dang gsung 
12b7(1): dang thugs rnams kyi// dkyil 'khor rab tu bshad par bya// lus ngag sems ni bsgoms pa yis// shes rab can gyi thig gdab pa// thig skud sar pa'i legs bskal ba// tshad ma rab tu mdzes 
13a1(1): pa yis// thugs kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa ste// khru ni bcu gnyis tshad du bya// ngos bzhi dang ni grwa bzhir ldan// sgo bzhi par ni rab tu brtags// de'i dbus su 'khor lo 
13a2(1): ni/ rab tu zlum por bri bar bya// de nas las kyi cho ga ni// mthong bas phyag rgya dgod par bya// de dbus rdo rje bri ba ni// in tra ni la'i kha dog 'dra// 'bar ba chen po rtsi lbu ba// 'jigs pa dag kyang 
13a3(1): rab 'jigs byed// 'khor lo chen po'i shar phyogs su// rdo rje 'bar bso rnam par brgyan// rin chen chen po'i lho pogs su// 'od zer mang po'i rab tu 'khrigs// pad+ma chen po nub phyogs su// pad+ma 
13a4(1): rag ga'i kha dog 'dra// ral gri chen po bang pogs su// 'od zer mang pos rab tu 'khrags// dbus na spyi dang 'dra bo 'od// spyan ni shar gyi gra ru bri// mA ma ki ni rigs 'byung ba'i// rdo rje de bzhin 
13a5(1): lho phyogs su// pad+ma kha phye dong bur btsos// nub phyogs su ni bri bar bya// ud pal mdzes pa byang phyogs su// mthing ka sprin dang 'dru bar bri// tho ba 'bar ba 'od gsal ba// shAr phyogs sgor ni 
13a6(1): bri baur bya// rdo rje 'bar sogs 'od bzang ba// be tson lho'i phyogs su bri// pad+ma 'bar ba'i 'od byed po// nub kyi phyogs su bri bar bya// rdo rje 'khyil ba rdo rje can// byang phyogs su ni bri bor bya// thugs 
13a7(1): kyi dkyil 'khor dam pa dang // yongs su gsal bar shes byas nas// lus dang ngag sems mchod pa yis// nan tan du ni mchod par bya// bud med rab tu mdongasau bzangs pa// lo grangs 
13b1(1): bcu drug lon pa ni// dri dang me tog 'breng brgyan te// yon tan skar mA ma kir// shes rab can gyis byin rlabs la// de'i dbus su mnyes par bya// sangs rgyas zhi ba'i gnas spros pa'i// nam mkha'i 
13b2(1): dbyings ni rab tu brgyan// gshang ci khu ba khrag la sogs// lha rnams la ni dbul bar byed// de lhor byas nas sangs rgyas dang // byang chub sems dpa' grags chen mnyes// de bzhin gshegs 
13b3(1): ba thams cad kyi sku dang gsung drang thugs kyi/ gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dkyil 'khor gyi le'u ste bzhi pa'o// 
13b4(1): de nas de bzhin gshegs pa ni// kun gyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi// rdo rje 'chang ba'i rgyal po ni// gnas kyi dbang phyug mchog gis// spyod pa kun mchog chos kyi don// spyod pa'i 
13b5(1): mtshan nyid bka' stsal to// rnam par mi rtog don las byung // 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug rigs// theg pa'i mchog ni bla med pa'i// dngos grub rab mchog sgrub par byed// 
13b6(1): rigs ngan smig ma mkhan la sogs// gsod don don gnyer sems dpa' rnams// theg chen bla na med pa yis// theg mchog 'di las 'grub par 'gyur// sems can mtshams 
13b7(1): med la sogs pa'i// sdig pa chen po byed pa yang // rdo rje theg pa rgya mtsho der// theg pa mchog ni 'di las grub// snying nas slob dpon smod pa dag/ sgrub dang 'grub par yong mi 'gyur// 
14a1(1): srog gcod pa'i sems can gang // brdzun du sbrul dga' ba dang // gzhan gyi nor la chags pa dang // rtag tu 'dod pa spyod pa dang // gA shad bci zas su za 
14a2(1): ste// de dag sgrub pa'i snod du 'gyur// ma dang sring mo bu mo la// 'dod pa pos ni mnyes byas nas// theg chen mchog gis chos nyid kyis// dngos grub rgya chen nges thob bo// sangs rgyas 
14a3(1):  sun sa / pa sa me gas te/ ma rtog rna/ nas sa sargyas 'grung bdu mgyur// denas skye ba ma sa ngan ma pa sel bas sogasag 
14a4(1): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur te/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag po ci'i slad dude bzhin gshegs 
14a5(1): ba thams cad kyi 'khor gyi nang du 'di lta bu'i tshig ngan pa gsung zhes gsol te// // de nas de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis/ sgrib pa thams cad 
14a6(1): rnam par sel ba la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rnams kyi tshig gsan nAs/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la 'di skad ces bka' stsal to// rigs kyi bu 'am 
14a7(1): mthong de skad ma zer cig/ snying po ye shes can rnams kyi// sangs rgyas chos nyid dag pa 'di// snying po chos kyi don las byung // byang chub spyod pa'i gnas 'di yin// de nas yang brjod 
14b1(1): kyis mi lang ba'i yang brjod kyi mi lang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing phra rab la sogs pa'i rdul phra mo srid kyi byang chub sems dpa' rnams 'jig skrag nas brgyal bar gyur to// de nas bcom ldan
14b2(1): 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag brgyal bar gyur pa gzigs nas/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi 
14b3(1): bdag po la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das byang chub sems dpa' chen po 'di dag bslang bar gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung 
14b4(1): dang thugs rdo rje de bzhin gshegs pas/ na mkha' dang mnyam pa gnyis su med pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs so// snyoms par zhugs ma thag tu bcom ldan 'das 
14b5(1): sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag pos 'od kyis reg pa tsam gyis/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de dag rang rang gi bstan la gnas par gyur to// de nas de bzhin 
14b6(1): gshegs pa thams cad ngo mtshar du gyur/ rmad du gyur/ dges pas khyad par du gyur nas/ chos kyi dbyings 'di skad ces gsol to// a ma'o chos e ma'i chos// e ma ho chos kyi 
14b7(1): don 'byung ba// chos don dag pa bdog med pa// rdo rje rgyal la phyag 'tshal 'dud// sku dang gsung thugs rab tu dag/ nam mkha' dag ni mnyam nyid gnas// rnam par mi 'gyur snang ba med// 
15a1(1): rdo rje sku la phyag 'tshal 'dud// thugs ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtso// dus gsum dag gi lam du byung // nam mkha' chen po dbyings gyur pa// nam kha'i lam du phyag 
15a2(1): 'tshal 'dud// na mkha'i sku las yang dag byung // na mkha'i lam la gnas pa'o// nam mkha'i thugs te chos kyi mchog/ spyod pa'i gnas la phyag 'tshal lo// 
15a3(1): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las/ kun tu spyod pa'i mchog gi le'u ste lnga pa'o// / de bzhin gshegs pa mi

15a5(1): sarba ta thA ga ta tsi tA badz+ra swa b+hA ba ad ma ko haM// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa rdo rje rnam par snang mdzad rdul dang bral ba'i gnas rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin lnga snyoms par zhugs 
15a6(1): nasasku byin gyis brlob pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA ga ta ka ya badz+ra swa b+ha wa ad ma ko haM// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa tshe dpag tu med pa mnyam pa nyid 
15a7(1): gnyis pa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ gsung byin gyis brlob pa'i sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA ga ta badz+ra swa b+ha ba ad ma ko ho// rdo rje gsum po de bzhin 
15b1(1): gshegs pa'i gsung // gnas ni gnas kyi rnam par sgom par bya// sngags kyi mtshan gyis shin tu mtshan byas la// mchog rab 'di yis sgrub pa nyid du bya// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin 
15b2(1): gshegs pa dkon mchog dpal ye shes sgron ma rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA ga ta a nu ra ga na badz+ra sa b+ha ba ad ma ko 
15b3(1): haM/ de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa grub pa gdon mi za ba rdo rje zhes bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhugs te/ sngags 'di gsungs so// oM sarba ta thA ga ta pu tsA badz+ra swa b+ha ba

16a1(1): ba rnam gsum sgrub par bya// lus dang ngag dang sems dmigs na// ngo bo nyid ni dmigs su med// sngags kyi lus su sbyor ba las// byang chub med cing bsgoms pa'ang med// 
16a2(1): sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan nyid du// 'di ni mdor na rnam dpyad nas// sngags kyis brtags pa'i tinge 'dzin// byang chub sbyor ba bsgom par bya// de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzin// de bzhin gshegs pa kun 
16a3(1): gyi mchod// sangs rgyas kun mchog kun mkhyen gyis// bsgoms pa'i mchog ni bka' stsal to// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas bor// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas
16a4(1): gzugs ni rab bsgoms nas// phra mo'i sbyor ba kun tu bsdum// sna'i rtse mor nyungs dkar bsam// 'gro dang mi 'gro nyungs dkar la// ye shes gnas ni nyams dga' ba// gsang ba'i ye shes 
16a5(1): kyis brtags bsgoms// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas sku'i gnas bsgoms te// de'i steng du gnas bzhag go// hUM na mkha'i 
16a6(1): dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// spyan gyi tshul du sbyor ba lnga// rdo rje pad+ma rnam par bsgom// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// rin tshon dkyil 
16a7(1): 'khor bsgom par bya// dang po sbyor ba'i nan tan gyis// de'i steng du yongs su bsgom// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// pad+ma'i dkyil 'khor sgom par bya// gsung gi rdo rje tshul sbyor bas// 
16b1(1): 'dod chags rdo rje can bsgom bya// na mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus gnas par// 'od kyi dkyil 'khor bsgom par bya// sangs rgyas tshul ni zhi bar spro// 'khor kyang khyad par bdag tu spro// ud dpal 'thing 
16b2(1): ka'i mdog 'dra ba// rtse mo lnga pa khyad par du// nas kyi 'bru tsam nan tan gyis// sna'i rtse mor rnam par bsam// tsa na ka yi 'bru tsam la// 'dab ma brgyad pa gi sar bcas// sna'i rtse mor 'di shes 
16b3(1): te// bsgoms pas byang chub gzhil bar 'gyur// 'khor lo la sogs khyad par du// bsgom pa de ni brtags par bya// dngos grub thams cad yon tan gnas// nyams dge' byang chub gnas
16b4(1): 'grub 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub gnas rnams ni// de ru mdor na spro bar bya// sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan pa yi// chos kyi tshigs rnams rab tu brjod// de nas dpal ldan rdo rje 'dzini// de nyid 
16b5(1): don kun ston pa pos// spyod pa kun mchog legs dag pa// gsang ba'i dam pa bka' stsal to// gzugs dang sgra dang ro ldan par// shes rab can gyis zla drug bsgom// gsang ba de nyid mchod 
16b6(1): chen gyis// legs par mchod nas bsgom par byas// dngos grub 'bras bu 'dod pa yis// zas su gshang btsi zos nas ni// sangs rgyas byang chub gnas rnams ni// yang dag bla med 'grub
16b7(1): bar 'gyur// zas su sha rnams bza' ba dang // sha chen dag ni rab brtags na// sku dang gsung dang thugs gsang ba'i// dngos grub thams cad 'grub par 'gyur// glang po'i sha dang rta'i sha/ 
17a1(1): de bzhin dam pa khyi'i sha// zas kyi phyir ni bza' bar bya// zas gzhan dag ni ma zos na// byang chub sems dpa' blo can dang // sangs rgyas rnams ni mnyes par 'gyur// 
17a2(1): 'di lta bu yis sbyor ba yis// myur du sangs rgyas nyid thob 'gyur// 'dod khams dbang phyug 'jig rten na// go 'bang las ni byed par 'gyur// gtso mo gzi can stobs dang ldan// mdangs
17a3(1): bzangs mthong na yid du 'ong // mthong ba tsam gyis bskul ba yis// 'jig rten 'di dag dbang du 'gyur// 'di na sangs rgyas thams cad kyi// gsang ba byang chub dam pa ste// yang dag sngags kyi 
17a4(1): gsang ba 'di// lus ngag sems las 'da' ba'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs kyi gsang ba gsang ba 'dus pa las/ sku gsung thugs byin gyis brlob pa'i

17a7(1): rgyas myur du thob par 'gyur// 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad ni// ji ltar 'dod par sten byas te// rang gi lha'i sbyor ba yis// bdag dang gzhan la mchod par bya// dka' thub sdom pa 
17b1(1): mi zad pas// bstan kyang grub par mi 'gyur gyi// 'dod pa'i longs spyod thams cad la// brten na myur du 'grub par 'gyur// slong mo za zhing mi bzlas te// ma bslad pa la cha mi bya// 'dod
17b2(1): ba kun la longs spyod cing // sngags kyi yan lag ma nyams bzlas// lus dang ngag dang sems rnams ni// bde bar gnas ni byang chub thob// gzhan du dus min 'chi ba dang // dmyal bar 
17b3(1): nges par bsreg par 'gyur// sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' dang // sngags kyi spyod pa spyod mchog rnams// chos mchog mi g.yo bsnyen pa yang // 'dod pa thams cad brten pas
